<script type="text/javascript">
//<![CDATA[
	function send(frm){
		if(frm.k.value.replace(/^(\s|\&nbsp;)*|(\s|\&nbsp;)*$/g,"")=='' || frm.k.value=='¿qué estás buscando?'){
			alert('Pero hombre... ¡escribe algo!');
			frm.k.value='';
			frm.k.focus();
			return false;
		}else if(frm.k.value.length<3){
			alert('Prueba con algo más largo, como mínimo de tres letras');
			frm.k.focus();
			return false;
		}

		if(!isNumeric($('#pricemin').val())){
			$('#pricemin').val('');
		}

		if(!isNumeric($('#pricemax').val())){
			$('#pricemax').val('');
		}

		
		return true;
	}
	
//]]>
</script>    
    
    
    
    <script type="text/javascript">
	function go(url){
		window.open('/_sc/go.php?'+url);
	}

	function details(url){
		document.location.href=url;
	}

	$(function() {
	    $("img.lazy").lazyload({
	    	 effect : "fadeIn"
		    });
	    
	});







	$(document).ready(function() {




		  

		 
		  var time = 7; // time in seconds
		 
		  var $progressBar,
		      $bar, 
		      $elem, 
		      isPause, 
		      tick,
		      percentTime;
		 
		    //Init the carousel
		    $("#owl-demo").owlCarousel({
		    	stopOnHover:true,
		      slideSpeed : 500,
		      paginationSpeed : 500,
		      singleItem : true,
		      afterInit : progressBar,
		      afterMove : moved,
		      startDragging : pauseOnDragging
		    });
		 
		    //Init progressBar where elem is $("#owl-demo")
		    function progressBar(elem){
		      $elem = elem;
		      //build progress bar elements
		      buildProgressBar();
		      //start counting
		      start();
		    }
		 
		    //create div#progressBar and div#bar then prepend to $("#owl-demo")
		    function buildProgressBar(){
		      $progressBar = $("<div>",{
		        id:"progressBar"
		      });
		      $bar = $("<div>",{
		        id:"bar"
		      });
		      $progressBar.append($bar).prependTo($elem);
		    }
		 
		    function start() {
		      //reset timer
		      percentTime = 0;
		      isPause = false;
		      //run interval every 0.01 second
		      tick = setInterval(interval, 10);
		    };
		 
		    function interval() {
		      if(isPause === false){
		        percentTime += 1 / time;
		        $bar.css({
		           width: percentTime+"%"
		         });
		        //if percentTime is equal or greater than 100
		        if(percentTime >= 100){
		          //slide to next item 
		          $elem.trigger('owl.next')
		        }
		      }
		    }
		 
		    //pause while dragging 
		    function pauseOnDragging(){
		      isPause = true;
		    }
		 
		    //moved callback
		    function moved(){
		      //clear interval
		      clearTimeout(tick);
		      //start again
		      start();
		    }
		 
		    //uncomment this to make pause on mouseover 
		    // $elem.on('mouseover',function(){
		    //   isPause = true;
		    // })
		    // $elem.on('mouseout',function(){
		    //   isPause = false;
		    // })


		    $('table:first','.popover-content').css('height',($('#content-right').outerHeight()-65)+'px');
		    //alert($('#content-right ').outerWidth());
		 
		});

</script>
    
    
    
    
    
    
    
    
    
    
    
    
    
    
    
    <script type="text/javascript">
//<![CDATA[		
	
		
	function go(url){
		window.open('/_sc/go.php?'+url);
	}
	
	function details(url,pos){
		$('#form-details').remove();
		$('<form>').attr({
		    action: url,
		    id: 'form-details',
		    method: 'post'
		}).appendTo('#content');

		$('<input>').attr({type: 'hidden',name:'page',value:''}).appendTo('#form-details');
		$('<input>').attr({type: 'hidden',name:'itempos',value:pos}).appendTo('#form-details');
		$('<input>').attr({type: 'hidden',name:'k',value:''}).appendTo('#form-details');
		$('<input>').attr({type: 'hidden',name:'cat1',value:'0'}).appendTo('#form-details');
		$('<input>').attr({type: 'hidden',name:'order',value:''}).appendTo('#form-details');

		$("#form-details").submit();
	}



	function buildURL(cat1){ 
		var frm = document.getElementById('filter_frm');
		base_url = 'http://www.bueni.es/search.php?';

		var cat1 = cat1 || $('#cat1').val();

		
		base_url = base_url + "cat1=" + cat1 + "&";

		
		base_url = base_url + "k=" + frm.elements["k"].value + "&";

		
		
		if(typeof(frm.elements["order"]) != "undefined" && frm.elements["order"].value != '' && frm.elements["order"].value != 0) {  
			base_url = base_url + "order=" + frm.elements["order"].value + "&" ; 
		}

		if(typeof(frm.elements["urlid"]) != "undefined" && frm.elements["urlid"].value != '' && frm.elements["urlid"].value != 0) {  
			base_url = base_url + "urlid=" + frm.elements["urlid"].value + "&" ; 
		}

		if(typeof(frm.elements["pricemin"]) != "undefined" && frm.elements["pricemin"].value != '' && frm.elements["pricemin"].value != 0) {  
			base_url = base_url + "pricemin=" + frm.elements["pricemin"].value + "&" ; 
		}

		if(typeof(frm.elements["pricemax"]) != "undefined" && frm.elements["pricemax"].value != '' && frm.elements["pricemax"].value != 0) {  
			base_url = base_url + "pricemax=" + frm.elements["pricemax"].value + "&" ; 
		}

		
		if(typeof(frm.elements["city"]) != "undefined" && frm.elements["city"].value != '') {  
			base_url = base_url + "city=" + frm.elements["city"].value + "&" ; 
		}
		

		if(typeof(frm.elements["r"]) != "undefined" && frm.elements["r"].value != '' && frm.elements["r"].value != 0) {  
			base_url = base_url + "r=" + frm.elements["r"].value + "&" ; 
		}		

		
		base_url = base_url.substr(0,base_url.length-1);
		document.location.href = base_url;
		return false; 
	}

	function changeFilterValues(_name,_value){
		var frm = document.getElementById('price_box');
		$('[name='+_name+']','#price_box').val(_value);
		$('#price_box').submit();
		return false;
	}

	

	
	//]]>
</script>

    </script>

    <script>

        var $menu = $(".dropdown-menu");

        // jQuery-menu-aim: <meaningful part of the example>
        // Hook up events to be fired on menu row activation.
        $menu.menuAim({
            activate: activateSubmenu,
            deactivate: deactivateSubmenu
        });
        // jQuery-menu-aim: </meaningful part of the example>

        // jQuery-menu-aim: the following JS is used to show and hide the submenu
        // contents. Again, this can be done in any number of ways. jQuery-menu-aim
        // doesn't care how you do this, it just fires the activate and deactivate
        // events at the right times so you know when to show and hide your submenus.
        function activateSubmenu(row) {
            var $row = $(row),
                submenuId = $row.data("submenuId"),
                $submenu = $("#" + submenuId),
                height = 'auto',
                width = $menu.outerWidth();

            // Show the submenu
            $submenu.css({
                display: "block",
                top: -1,
                left: width - 3,  // main should overlay submenu
                height: height - 4  // padding for main dropdown's arrow
            });

            // Keep the currently activated row's highlighted look
            $row.find("a").addClass("maintainHover");
        }

        function deactivateSubmenu(row) {
        	var $row = $(row),
                submenuId = $row.data("submenuId"),
                $submenu = $("#" + submenuId);

            // Hide the submenu and remove the row's highlighted look
            $submenu.css("display", "none");
            $row.find("a").removeClass("maintainHover");
        }

        // Bootstrap's dropdown menus immediately close on document click.
        // Don't let this event close the menu if a submenu is being clicked.
        // This event propagation control doesn't belong in the menu-aim plugin
        // itself because the plugin is agnostic to bootstrap.

        
        $(".dropdown-menu li").mouseenter(function() {
			activateSubmenu(this);
        });
        
        $(".dropdown-menu li").mouseleave(function() {
			deactivateSubmenu(this);
        });
        
        $('.popover').mouseleave(function() {
        	deactivateSubmenu();
        });
        
        

    </script>
